<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>скачка</a> (9837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Horse-racing-4.jpg/220px-Horse-racing-4.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="183" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Horse-racing-4.jpg/330px-Horse-racing-4.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Horse-racing-4.jpg/440px-Horse-racing-4.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1061" data-file-height="884" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>скачка</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>ска́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skáčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>ска́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>ска́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>ска́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gallop</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> horse races</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> download (file transfer to the local computer)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скачок.html>скачо́к</a> (11077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скакать.html>скака́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skakátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачок.html>скачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>скачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>скачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скачок.html>скачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jump, bound, leap; surge</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">square</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сквер.html>сквер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skver</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сквер.html>скве́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сквер.html>скве́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сквер.html>скве́ров</a></b>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скверный.html>скве́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skvérnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скверне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)скверне́й</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозить.html>сквози́ть</a> (12646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skvozʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сквозить.html>сквози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skvozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сквозить.html>сквози́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ <b>skvozít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a draught here; there is a draft here</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to show [be seen] through
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сквозить.html>сквози́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:занавеска.html>занаве́ску</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svet <b>skvozít</b> čerez zanavésku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">light shines [is seen] through the curtain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to show, to be discernible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:манера.html>мане́рах</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сквозить.html>сквози́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самонадеянность.html>самонаде́янность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jevó manérax <b>skvozít</b> nékotoraja samonadejannostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a hint of presumption in his manner</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(cloth)</i> to be transparent, to be threadbare</li></ol>

***скидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a> (21491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">скид-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skid-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw down, to throw off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skídyvatʹ</b> sneg s krýši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>throw</b> the snow <b>off</b> the roof</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(clothes, shoes)</i> to take off, to throw off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw off, to dethrone</li>
<li>to throw together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́чу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skídyvatʹ</b> v kúču</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pile; heap</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock off, to discount</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to copy <i>(to)</i>, to e-mail <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skídyvatʹ</b> na disk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to save to a disk</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нуть</a> (5725)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw down, to throw off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>Конь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нул</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:седок.html>седока́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Konʹ <b>skínul</b> sedoká.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The horse <b>threw off</b> its rider.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skínutʹ</b> sneg s krýši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>throw</b> the snow <b>off</b> the roof</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(clothes, shoes)</i> to take off, to throw off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нул</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:ботинок.html>боти́нки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>skínul</b> (s sebjá) botínki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he kicked off his shoes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw off, to dethrone</li>
<li>to throw together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock off, to discount</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to copy <i>(to)</i>, to e-mail <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>Ски́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почтовый.html>почто́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ящик.html>я́щик</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skinʹ</b> telefón na moj počtóvyj jáščik.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">E-mail the telephone number to my mailbox.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирда́</a> (17617)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skirdá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>ски́рды</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(hay) stack, rick</li></ol>

<p><b>скир<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да́</a></b>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1b: мн. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирды́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирда́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирда́ми</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:скирда.html>скирда́х</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скиснуть.html>ски́снуть</a> (19341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киснуть.html>ки́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kísnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скиснуть.html>ски́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skísnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:киснуть.html>ки́снуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">скиса́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn sour (e.g. a milk product)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become sad or depressed</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***скитаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скитаться.html>скита́ться</a> (18388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">скытати ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skytati sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with Serbian Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">скытати сѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skytati sę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">скита́тися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skytátysja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:скит.html>ски́там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skítam se</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ски́тати <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">skítati sе</i>. More distantly cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kutė́ti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skundа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">scuddian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shake, to push</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">scutten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shake, to push</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скитаться.html>скита́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skitátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to wander, to stray
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скитаться.html>скита́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> бе́лу <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skitatʹsja po bélu svétu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock about the world</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ски<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>та́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — поскитаться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-скит-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скиф.html>скиф</a> (28558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скиф.html>скиф</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skif</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скиф.html>ски́фа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скиф.html>ски́фы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скиф.html>ски́фов</a></b>)

***склад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склад</a> (1936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склад</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sklad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>скла́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>скла́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>скла́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>warehouse, storehouse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> depot, dump</li>
<li>constitution, disposition, turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склад</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sklad</b> umá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cast of mind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>breed</li>
<li>way <i>(of life)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> harmony</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sense</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> syllable (in this sense, the plurals have the endings accented)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čitátʹ po <b>skladám</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read by syllables</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склад</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хранилище.html>храни́лище</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> жарг. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>прост</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1c : мн. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склады́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>складо́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́ми</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́х</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>местный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a> ед. ч.: (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>складу́</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строй</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:характер.html>хара́ктер</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1a−: мн. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуются</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>слог</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1c: мн. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склады́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>складо́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́ми</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>склада́х</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-клад-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склад.html>скла́д</a>(ывать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sklád(yvatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складка.html>скла́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skládka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складка.html>скла́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складка.html>скла́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:складка.html>скла́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crease, buckling, crimp, fold, plica, ply</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-клад-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.
